msg:The hotel is in a good location. It takes about five minutes to walk to Raffles Chaotianmen and about ten minutes to Jiefangbei. Downstairs is Chaotianmen Station of Line 1. It is also convenient to take a taxi. Although there are many hotels in the same building, the elevator of Voco is independent. , the room is very quiet.
The only drawback is that the landmark river view room in the picture of the package I booked this time has a bed, but in fact it does not. The so-called landmark river view is probably a small section of the Yangtze River between residential buildings. I think there is no need to upgrade to a room with a landmark river view.
The room is clean, but it is stuffy. The central air conditioner controls the room temperature. It is 15 or 16 degrees outside and 28 degrees in the room. There is a half-open window for ventilation... It is my first time in Chongqing and I don't know if this is a common problem. The bathroom in the room was okay. I thought the ventilation was not good enough, but the water vapor didn't drift out of the shower room when I took a shower. In addition, the disposable toothpaste provided is quite unique and niceüëç.
Finally, the best thing is that the hotel's breakfast is quite rich and the waiters are very enthusiastic. However, the view of the landmark river view cannot be complimented and I cannot give it full 5 stars.

msg:Is Chongqing Chaotianmen VOCO Hotel really a five-star hotel? This is the biggest doubt of my trip to Chongqing. This hotel is also the only mine I stepped on in Chongqing. I would like to share some of my personal feelings with you, hoping to provide some reference for you! 
1. I have a right to upgrade from a superior river view room to a deluxe river view room for free in my Ctrip order, but the hotel did not mention it at all when I checked in. 
2. On the day of check-in, because I brought my child, I needed an extra pair of slippers, so I called the front desk to send a pair of slippers. It was such a simple service, but I called three times in succession and it took an hour to deliver it to me. 
3. The hotel room faces the street and is very noisy at night. On the first night, I thought the window was not closed tightly. The next day, I saw that the window was tightly closed. I have stayed in so many five-star hotels, and I have also stayed in street-facing ones, but this is the first time I have encountered such poor sound insulation of the windows. 
4. For breakfast on the first day, we went downstairs at 9:40, but there was nothing left at the noodle stall, only rice noodles were available. I ordered two bowls of porridge at the porridge stall, but they didn‚Äôt make it for me in 20 minutes. I went to ask them to tell me that they were making it (in fact, I saw that the waiter gave my porridge to another person). I complained to the manager, and the guest at the next table said that he grabbed the last wonton, and he also felt that the catering service arrangement was unreasonable.
5. Ctrip says that the room area is 32-35 square meters, but I personally feel that it is not, and it is the first time I have encountered a five-star hotel without a bathtub.
6. The bathing water is hot and cold, and it is scalding when it is hot. The waiter explained that it is hot water provided by the property, and they have no way to deal with it.
7. The air conditioning temperature in the room cannot be adjusted. If the air conditioning is turned on at night, it can reach 31‚ÑÉ, and it is cold when it is not turned on. The child did not sleep well for three nights.
8. Add a question about the restaurant. When I went there, there were no clean seats, so I sat in an uncleaned seat, and then told the waiter to clean it. The waiter was cleaning a table next to me at the time, so I went to get the meal. As a result, when I came back after getting the meal, my table was not cleaned yet. I got angry, and the waiter came to clean it.
9. Such a big hotel only has a receptionist, but no porter. I can't understand it.
After staying for two nights, I was a little intolerable, so I complained to Ctrip. The hotel's attitude was good, and they offered to upgrade me to a deluxe river view room, but I only had one night left, and I didn't want to toss it, and I didn't complain to blackmail him. These problems can't be solved by upgrading a room. When I checked out, the front desk manager insisted on giving me a gift, and I politely declined. I can understand the manager's mood, but to be honest, I didn't expect that such a high-end brand like InterContinental would have a hotel with such a big gap in service and conditions. I was very disappointed, really disappointed, so I couldn't accept any gifts from the hotel. If I accepted it, I couldn't objectively state my experience. I hope my statement can help others, don't step on thunder!
Finally, the hotel is not without merits. I will mention two points: first, the location is particularly advantageous, in the core area of ‚Äã‚ÄãChaotianmen, and the transportation is very convenient. Second, the attitude of the staff is good, and they have all the etiquette that a five-star hotel should have.
